  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_a3dccb9c-a37c-4426-acda-f56ff5843c55'
      });

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer12388528865896212993">Sang Pemimpi adalah sebuah lantunan kisah kehidupan yang memesona dan akan membuat Anda percaya akan tenaga cinta, percaya pada kekuatan mimpi dan pengorbanan, lebih dari itu, akan membuat Anda percaya kepada Tuhan. Andrea akan membawa Anda berkelana menerobos sudut-sudut pemikiran di mana Anda akan menemukan pandangan yang berbeda tentang nasib, tantangan intelektualitas,</span>
  <span id="freeText12388528865896212993" style="display:none">Sang Pemimpi adalah sebuah lantunan kisah kehidupan yang memesona dan akan membuat Anda percaya akan tenaga cinta, percaya pada kekuatan mimpi dan pengorbanan, lebih dari itu, akan membuat Anda percaya kepada Tuhan. Andrea akan membawa Anda berkelana menerobos sudut-sudut pemikiran di mana Anda akan menemukan pandangan yang berbeda tentang nasib, tantangan intelektualitas, dan kegembiraan yang meluap-luap, sekaligus kesedihan yang mengharu biru. <br /><br />Tampak komikal pada awalnya, selayaknya kenakalan remaja biasa, tapi kemudian tanpa Anda sadari, kisah dan karakter-karakter dalam buku ini lambat laun menguasai Anda. Karena potret-potret kecil yang menawan akan menghentakkan Anda pada rasa humor yang halus namun memiliki efek filosofis yang meresonansi. Karena arti perjuangan hidup dalam kemiskinan yang membelit dan cita-cita yang gagah berani dalam kisah dua orang tokoh utama buku ini: Arai dan Ikal akan menuntun Anda dengan semacam keanggunan dan daya tarik agar Anda dapat melihat ke dalam diri sendiri dengan penuh pengharapan, agar Anda menolak semua keputusasaan dan ketakberdayaan Anda sendiri. <br /><br />“Kita tak kan pernah mendahului nasib!” teriak Arai.<br />“Kita akan sekolah ke Prancis, menjelajahi Eropa sampai ke Afrika! Apa pun yang terjadi!”<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12388528865896212993" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1728768249" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer925212706837294616"><i>Sang Pemimpi (The Dreamer)</i> is a second book of <i>Laskar Pelangi</i> tetralogy <i>(The Rainbow Troops)</i>. The novel is written by adored Indonesian author, Andrea Hirata.<br/><br/>It tells a story about Ikal (Andrea Hirata himself), Arai, and Jimbron. Ikal, a smart and popular student in the school, befriended kind-hearted Jimbron and his cousin Arai. Arai is the main protagonist of the novel, the dreamer, the visionary, who always think for others first before himself.<br/><br/>After finishing secondary school, the trio went </span>
  <span id="freeText925212706837294616" style="display:none"><i>Sang Pemimpi (The Dreamer)</i> is a second book of <i>Laskar Pelangi</i> tetralogy <i>(The Rainbow Troops)</i>. The novel is written by adored Indonesian author, Andrea Hirata.<br /><br />It tells a story about Ikal (Andrea Hirata himself), Arai, and Jimbron. Ikal, a smart and popular student in the school, befriended kind-hearted Jimbron and his cousin Arai. Arai is the main protagonist of the novel, the dreamer, the visionary, who always think for others first before himself.<br /><br />After finishing secondary school, the trio went to nearby town to continue their study. There, they go through the hardship of life: they attend class from morning to afternoon, then need to work till late at night to pay for their living costs. Although exhausted from daily routine, they support each other and keep their dreams burning in their heart.<br /><br />Light and humorous at first, the story then touches the readers' heart as the trio struggle and fight their way to their dreams. A fun and heart-warming read, Andrea Hirata once again written a wonderful novel as good as his first novel, <i>Laskar Pelangi</i>.<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://gerryvyers.wordpress.com/2016/08/30/sang-pemimpi">https://gerryvyers.wordpress.com/2016...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="925212706837294616" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3039052242" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3039052242" />
    <a title="Dwi Putri" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/99521759-dwi-putri"><img alt="Dwi Putri" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1590821672p2/99521759.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3039052242?book_show_action=true">Nov 07, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dwi Putri" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dwi Putri" href="/user/show/99521759-dwi-putri">Dwi Putri</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3039052242" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10718800576543396759">"Dream on, then God will embrace your dreams." - Andrea Hirata<br/><br/>'Sang Pemimpi' by Andrea Hirata is a tetralogy of the novel 'Laskar Pelangi' which tells about Ikal and Arai who have dreams of being able to continue their studies at the Univesite de Paris, Sorbonne, France. In the beginning, that sibling (from another parent) were motivated by their teacher in high school, Mr. Belia, who told about the university in France. The poverty suffered by the two brothers didn't prevent them from sticking </span>
  <span id="freeText10718800576543396759" style="display:none">"Dream on, then God will embrace your dreams." - Andrea Hirata<br /><br />'Sang Pemimpi' by Andrea Hirata is a tetralogy of the novel 'Laskar Pelangi' which tells about Ikal and Arai who have dreams of being able to continue their studies at the Univesite de Paris, Sorbonne, France. In the beginning, that sibling (from another parent) were motivated by their teacher in high school, Mr. Belia, who told about the university in France. The poverty suffered by the two brothers didn't prevent them from sticking to their dreams. Until arriving at the end of high school they both decided to migrate to Jakarta. Ikal decided to become an employee at a post office that required to have excellent physical condition, while Arai, due to limitations in her lungs, decided to look for work that was not the same as Ikal, he decided to look for work in Kalimantan. Until finally in the following year after graduation they both could continue their studies with their own labors, Ikal was accepted to study at the University of Indonesia, while Arai decided to study at Mulawarman University. At the end of the end of graduation a scholarship was opened to continue the master's study. Ikal and Arai were reunited in the scholarship selection. And in the end they were both accepted to continue their master studies with scholarships at the Univesite de Paris, Sorbonne, France.<br /><br />'Sang Pemimpi' contains a moral lesson:<br />• Obedience to worship God is very important.<br />• Basically we don't need someone who has a lot of theories but no practice at all.<br />• School didn't teach things what we have to think about, but it teaches us how to think.<br />• The most friendly professional groups are musicians, the most ignorant are politicians, and the most annoying is the book publisher.<br />• Without dreams and enthusiasm people will die.<br />• Run will make our minds relax.<br />• Hygiene is part of faith.<br />• Where there is a will, there is a way.<br />• Difficulties from all difficulties in life are a part of something the perfect order and the surest nature of the this solar system.<br />• The young people we need are capable people<br />dream of something that no one has ever dreamed of.<br />• Basically we should be able to see the beauty behind something, beauty which only people normally encounter in dreams (that is a true dreamer, a true dreamer).<br />• Smoking makes the eyes cloudy (teach us to healthy life).<br />• The best achievement is being able to make parents happy and proud. <br />• This novel also teaches us to not give up.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10718800576543396759" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3641274210" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3641274210" />
    <a title="Bethari Bunga" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/124109117-bethari-bunga"><img alt="Bethari Bunga" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1604553184p2/124109117.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3641274210?book_show_action=true">Nov 12, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bethari Bunga" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bethari Bunga" href="/user/show/124109117-bethari-bunga">Bethari Bunga</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/124109117-bethari-bunga?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/124109117-bethari-bunga?shelf=indonesian">indonesian</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3641274210" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15689296036131544598">As written on the title, this is <i>“novel yang menggugah semangat”</i> (a novel that sparks hope, or is generally inspiring). <b> This novel portrays hope and dreams, at the intersection of poverty and social issues.</b> As Ikal said, “What’s the point of me studying a binomial theory to count infinite numbers, while what’s infinite for me is the impossibility to continue my study beyond high school?” he added, “Tell God about your dream, so that He will laugh at it!” (page 145) 💰<br/><br/>Moreover, Andrea successfull</span>
  <span id="freeText15689296036131544598" style="display:none">As written on the title, this is <i>“novel yang menggugah semangat”</i> (a novel that sparks hope, or is generally inspiring). <b> This novel portrays hope and dreams, at the intersection of poverty and social issues.</b> As Ikal said, “What’s the point of me studying a binomial theory to count infinite numbers, while what’s infinite for me is the impossibility to continue my study beyond high school?” he added, “Tell God about your dream, so that He will laugh at it!” (page 145) 💰<br /><br />Moreover, Andrea successfully delivered <b>a painful social commentary, in a way that makes us laugh in irony</b>. In a story about Capo Lam Nyet Pho, who embodied the idea of <i>“possibility”</i> and <i>“where there is a will, there is a way”</i>, Ikal praised Capo for her ability to put thoughts into practice. Ikal said, “Making ideas into reality should be considered to be a new course in our school system.” (page 165) 🗣<br /><br />Furthermore, in a world where reality doesn’t always meet our expectation, it’s hard to feel motivated all the time. <b>It’s easier to associate <i>“being realistic”</i> with <i>“seeing life in a pessimistic worldview”.</i></b> Ikal argued, “Being realistic is a brake that stops people from dreaming (page 144).” The rest of the story discusses his standpoint to see his dreams of exploring the realm of possibilities, in the face of reality of being a poor guy living in Belitong, Indonesia. It was a long story until Ikal came to a realization that, “Doing the best thing you can do right now, is the most realistic thing ever”. It’s referred in the novel that, “If people’s enthusiasm toward life is a curve, then optimism is what keeps it going up.” (page 208) 📈<br /><br />Or, as Arai said, <b>“Without hope, <i>people like us</i> will die!”.</b> 🙌🏻<br /><br /><b>To sum up, I highly recommend this book to anyone feeling demotivated at any stage of life. The <i>esprit de corps</i> shared in the story really uplifts me.</b> For me, this is Andrea Hirata’s masterpiece after “Ayah”. I always have this book on my bedside table, and I lost count how many times I have read this book in my life! Also, P.S: This review is written with my own version of its English translation, thus I recommend you to get an official English one. 📚<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15689296036131544598" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer15105407621893730767">SANG PEMIMPI is the second book of Laskar Pelangi tetralogy. This novel tells Ikal with his high school years since his little friend Arai and Jimbron. Arai is a distant brother Ikal is an orphan and is the last family member who is still alive and eventually became the foster brother Ikal. Jimbron is an orphan who was obsessed with horses and stutter when I'm enthusiastic about something or when nervous. All three were friends since childhood until they go to school in SMA Manggar, the first hi</span>
  <span id="freeText15105407621893730767" style="display:none">SANG PEMIMPI is the second book of Laskar Pelangi tetralogy. This novel tells Ikal with his high school years since his little friend Arai and Jimbron. Arai is a distant brother Ikal is an orphan and is the last family member who is still alive and eventually became the foster brother Ikal. Jimbron is an orphan who was obsessed with horses and stutter when I'm enthusiastic about something or when nervous. All three were friends since childhood until they go to school in SMA Manggar, the first high school that stood on the eastern Belitong. Because far from home three of them that lived in a shack fish market. Attend school in the morning and work as porters fish at the port in the early morning. They have a very fierce headmaster named Mr. Mustar. Arai is a friend of Ikal who always invites her friends to do crazy things, including watching the hot movies in theaters, which eventually caught by Mr. Mustar who previously had fugitive Mr. Mustar. But Arai is also that invites them both to dare to dream. Includes dream to go to Sourbone France. Various efforts have been made Arai and Ikal to get a scholarship to Sourbone. And finally Ikal and Arai are going to study in Jakarta, which ultimately makes them both separately but can still meet in France. Independent living separately from their parents with the background economic conditions are very limited but has a big goal, a goal which, when viewed from the background of their lives, just a dream. Now that dream come true, only with a capital of dreams and the spirit of Arai and Ikal could reach his master's degree in French.<br />For those of you who already read the novel Laskar Pelangi, you can not miss novel on this one because this is a continuation of Laskar Pelangi novel. In this novel will tell how the struggle Ikal and Arai to go to France.<br /></span>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText9322537416363554140" style="display:none"> usually write a review of Indonesian's books in Bahasa Indonesia, but in this case, I really want THE WHOLE WORLD to know this novel.<br />Despite the fact that I havent read Laskar Pelangi yet, which is the first novel written by Andrea Hirata (this one is his 2nd), but I didnt have a hard time understanding the plot. This book tells a story of the writer when he was still a High School student in Belitong. With a strong Melayu influence, Andrea tells his story unlike any other.<br />I can only give 2 words to describe this book:<br />ABSOLUTELY SUPPERB!!!!<br />There are lots of important life lessons that we can get from this book, and we are also forced - in a good way - to look at the way we live right now, where we stand, and the things that we've been taking for granted for a long time.<br /><br />I really wish this book can be translated to english and be imported, because I really want EVERYBODY to know and learn something from this book.<br /><br /><br />Andrea Hirata, you rock. Magnifique!<br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer34546483" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer306302246521102198">I recommend anyone that has lack in confidence about the future and what he/she can or cannot do, read this book. Andrea is successful in proving that we need a dream, a goal in life. <br/><br/>I often tell my friends that if you reach for the skyscraper, you might only reach the roof of you house; if you reach higher to the sky, you might get to the highest end of the skyscraper; so you have to reach for the stars, so you would at least reach the sky. Dream... and live up to it. </span>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('WzPMR06+ZE97tnJZ8Q1L61O1tEMsMEdMmTaC7cyM92bsUEScHN6J/kXgG3VWSLKVErASqKOdIHy3N7kTL9B31w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('kbwMrBHCw1wgC8jzc9aQHl3y98YXc/hqJkr1CnT5HVEm34R3Q6Iu7R5dod/Uk2lgHPdRLZjen1oIS870l6Wd4A==')})
  }

//<![CDATA[
      var newTip = new Tip($('bookCover_6688121'), "\n\n  <h2><a class=\"readable bookTitle\" href=\"https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6688121-negeri-5-menara?from_choice=false&amp;from_home_module=false\">Negeri 5 Menara<\/a><\/h2>\n\n      <div>\n        by <a class=\"authorName\" href=\"/author/show/3012699.Ahmad_Fuadi?a=9&amp;origin=related_works\">Ahmad Fuadi<\/a><span title=\"Goodreads Author!\">*<\/span>\n      <\/div>\n\n          <div class=\"smallText uitext darkGreyText\">\n            <span class=\"minirating\"><span class=\"stars staticStars notranslate\"><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p3\"><\/span><\/span> 4.10 avg rating &mdash; 12,010 ratings<\/span>            &mdash; published 2009\n          <\/div>\n\n    <div class=\"addBookTipDescription\">\n      \n<span id=\"freeTextContainer9293287504126207554\">Alif lahir di pinggir Danau Maninjau dan tidak pernah menginjak tanah di luar ranah Minangkabau. Masa kecilnya adalah berburu durian runtuh di rimba Bukit Barisan, bermain bola di sawah berlumpur dan tentu mandi berkecipak di air biru Danau Maninjau.<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText9293287504126207554\" style=\"display:none\">Alif lahir di pinggir Danau Maninjau dan tidak pernah menginjak tanah di luar ranah Minangkabau. Masa kecilnya adalah berburu durian runtuh di rimba Bukit Barisan, bermain bola di sawah berlumpur dan tentu mandi berkecipak di air biru Danau Maninjau.\n\nTiba-tiba saja dia harus naik bus tiga hari tiga malam melintasi punggung Sumatera dan Jawa menuju sebuah desa di pelosok Jawa Timur. Ibunya ingin dia menjadi Buya Hamka walau Alif ingin menjadi Habibie. Dengan setengah hati dia mengikuti perintah Ibunya: belajar di pondok.\n\nDi kelas hari pertamanya di Pondok Madani (PM), Alif terkesima dengan “mantera” sakti man jadda wajada. Siapa yang bersungguh-sungguh pasti sukses.\n\nDia terheran-heran mendengar komentator sepakbola berbahasa Arab, anak menggigau dalam bahasa Inggris, merinding mendengar ribuan orang melagukan Syair Abu Nawas dan terkesan melihat pondoknya setiap pagi seperti melayang di udara.\n\nDipersatukan oleh hukuman jewer berantai, Alif berteman dekat dengan Raja dari Medan, Said dari Surabaya, Dulmajid dari Sumenep, Atang dari Bandung dan Baso dari Gowa. Di bawah menara masjid yang menjulang, mereka berenam kerap menunggu maghrib sambil menatap awan lembayung yang berarak pulang ke ufuk. Di mata belia mereka, awan-awan itu menjelma menjadi negara dan benua impian masing-masing. Kemana impian jiwa muda ini membawa mereka? Mereka tidak tahu. Yang mereka tahu adalah: Jangan pernah remehkan impian, walau setinggi apa pun. Tuhan sungguh Maha Mendengar.\n\nBagaimana perjalanan mereka ke ujung dunia ini dimulai? Siapa horor nomor satu mereka? Apa pengalaman mendebarkan di tengah malam buta di sebelah sungai tempat jin buang anak? Bagaimana sampai ada yang kasak-kusuk menjadi mata-mata misterius? Siapa Princess of Madani yang mereka kejar-kejar? Kenapa mereka harus botak berkilat-kilat? Bagaimana sampai Icuk Sugiarto, Arnold Schwarzenegger, Ibnu Rusyd, bahkan Maradona sampai akhirnya ikut campur? Ikuti perjalanan hidup yang inspiratif ini langsung dari mata para pelakunya. Negeri Lima Menara adalah buku pertama dari sebuah trilogi.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"9293287504126207554\" href=\"#\" onclick=\"swapContent(\$(this));; return false;\">...more<\/a>\n\n <div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer528142188101066570">Under a bright sunny sky, the three-day Byron Bay Writers’ Festival welcomed Andrea Hirata who charmed audiences with his modesty and gracious behavior during two sessions. <br/><br/>Andrea also attended a special event where he and Tim Baker, an Australian surfing writer, spoke to a gathering of several hundred school children. During one session, Andrea was on a panel with Pulitzer Prize winning journalis</span>
  <span id="freeText528142188101066570" style="display:none">Under a bright sunny sky, the three-day Byron Bay Writers’ Festival welcomed Andrea Hirata who charmed audiences with his modesty and gracious behavior during two sessions. <br /><br />Andrea also attended a special event where he and Tim Baker, an Australian surfing writer, spoke to a gathering of several hundred school children. During one session, Andrea was on a panel with Pulitzer Prize winning journalist from Washington, DC, Katharine Boo, which he said was a great honor.<br /><br />The August event for the school children was very meaningful to Andrea, the barefooted boy from <br />Belitung, as he made mental comparisons with the educational opportunities of these children, compared to what he experienced. <br /><br />And now his own life story is about to become even more amazing, as his book Laskar Pelangi (The Rainbow Troops) is being published around the world in no less than twenty-four countries and in 12 languages. It has caught the eye of some of the world’s top publishing houses, such as Penguin, Random House, Farrar, Straus and Giroux, (New York, US) and many others. Translations are already on sale in Brazil, Taiwan, South Korea and Malaysia. <br /><br />All this has come about because of the feeling of appreciation that the young Andrea felt for his teacher, Muslimah. He promised her that he’d write a book for her someday. This was because for him and his school friends, a book was the most valuable thing they could think of. <br /><br />Andrea told a story that illustrated this fact. When royalties flowed in for him he decided to give his community a library. He spent a lot of money on books. He left the village headman in charge of administering the library. However, when he came back several months later, all the books were gone. People loved the books, but they had no concept of how a lending library functioned. <br /><br />“Some of them could not even read, but they just loved to have a book, an object of great value and importance, in their homes. We will restock the library with books and this time it will be run by our own administration,” he laughed.<br /><br />Andrea told this story as we sat in the coffee shop adjoining a Gold Coast City Library, one of 12 scattered around the city. One of the librarians, Jenneth Duque, showed him around the library, including the new state-of-the-art book sorting machine, for processing returns located in the staff area. As he saw the books being returned through pigeonholes by the borrowers and the computerized conveyor belt sorting them into the correct bin for reshelving, the sight made him laugh and prompted the telling of that story.<br /><br />Andrea wrote the book for his teacher while in the employ of Telkom, but the completed manuscript was taken from his room, which was located in a Bandung student accommodation community. Whoever took the manuscript knew enough to send it to a publisher and that’s how Andrea, an unhappy postal service worker who had studied economics in Europe and the UK, became the accidental author of the biggest selling novel in Indonesia’s history.<br /><br />He has since written seven more books. <br /><br />Fast forward to 2011 and Andrea was in Iowa, the US, where he did a reading of his short story, The Dry Season. He was approached by an independent literary agent, Kathleen Anderson. They talked, but for six months there was no news until an email arrived telling him that one of the best publishers in the US, Farrar, Straus and Giroux, had accepted his book. <br /><br />Then every week, more publishers said “yes” and now he has 24 contracts from the world’s leading publishers.<br /><br />Andrea worked with Angie Kilbane of the US on the English translations of Laskar Pelangi and its sequel Sang Pemimpi (The Dreamer). Translators from several other countries have visited his home village in Belitung to do research. <br /><br />“For a long time I wondered what was the key to the enormous success of my book,” Andrea said. <br /><br />“I think there’s no single right answer. Perhaps people are fed up with writing focused on urban issues or esca</span>
  <a data-text-id="528142188101066570" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
